(22, 'series_grinder_pipeline_component', 'batch_pipeline', 'series_extraction', 'pipeline', '# Series Grinder Pipeline Guide (Steps 1–7)\r\n\r\n**Component:** Series Grinder Pipeline (PowerShell)\r\n**Domain:** Content Extraction, Batch Processing\r\n**Topic:** Series Metadata Extraction, File Processing\r\n**Unit Type:** Batch Pipeline\r\n**Created:** 2026-02-02\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## Overview\r\nThe Series Grinder pipeline is a multi-step PowerShell batch process that extracts, normalizes, and cleans series metadata from raw provider payloads. Each step is a dedicated script, operating on files only (no DB writes), producing intermediate JSON artifacts for later ingestion.\r\n\r\n## Key Scripts & Steps\r\n- `series_grinder.ps1` – Extracts core series fields from raw payloads\r\n- `series_grinder_2_series_ext.ps1` – Extracts extended series metadata\r\n- `series_grinder_3_seasons.ps1` – Extracts season units by structure\r\n- `series_grinder_4_season_ext.ps1` – Extracts extended season metadata\r\n- `series_grinder_5_episodes.ps1` – Extracts episode units, supports fallback for season-keyed objects\r\n- `series_grinder_6_cleaner.ps1` – Cleans up processed files and removes raw artifacts\r\n- `series_grinder_7_finalizer.ps1` – (Empty/placeholder for future finalization)\r\n- `series_grinder_arrays.ps1` – Handles array-based series payloads, repairs display wrapping\r\n\r\n## Key Workflows\r\n- Each script reads from `raw_store/pickup/default` and writes to `series_sep/`\r\n- Extraction is anchor-based, not schema-based (brace/bracket block parsing)\r\n- No DB access; all operations are file-based for safety and traceability\r\n- Cleaning step removes all intermediate and raw artifacts\r\n\r\n## Integration Points\r\n- Downstream: Normalizer and ingest workers\r\n- Upstream: Provider payload downloaders\r\n\r\n## CVI/Registry Notes\r\n- All scripts are modular and CVI-explicit for registry onboarding\r\n- Each step is independently runnable for debugging\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## Actionable Onboarding\r\n- Run: Execute each script in order for a full pipeline\r\n- Registry: All modules are CVI-ready for PCDE_memory onboarding\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:49:07', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

(51, 'embedding_pipeline_worker', 'content_enrichment', 'embedding_vectorization', 'worker', '# MiraTV Embedding Pipeline Worker Guide\r\n\r\n## Component: embedding_pipeline.ps1\r\n\r\n### Purpose\r\nAutomates the embedding pipeline for series, VOD, or live content in the MiraTV ingest system. This worker script is responsible for triggering embedding jobs, managing input/output files, and coordinating with downstream AI or vectorization services.\r\n\r\n### Location\r\n`C:/miratv_ingest/workers/embedding_pipeline.ps1`\r\n\r\n### Operational Context\r\n- **Domain:** Content Enrichment / Vectorization\r\n- **Trigger:** Manual or orchestrated via spine scheduler or batch triggers\r\n- **Inputs:** Processed content files (JSON, text, or other supported formats)\r\n- **Outputs:** Embedding vectors, logs, and status reports (typically in `processed/` or `tmp/`)\r\n- **Downstream:** May call external AI embedding APIs (Cohere, OpenAI) or local embedding workers\r\n\r\n### Usage Pattern\r\n- Run as part of the enrichment phase after grinder/normalization\r\n- Can be invoked directly or by orchestration scripts in `triggers/` or `spine/`\r\n- Supports parameterized input (e.g., target file, embedding model)\r\n\r\n### Key Steps\r\n1. **Input Validation:** Checks for required input files and parameters\r\n2. **Embedding Job Launch:** Calls embedding service or script, passing content for vectorization\r\n3. **Output Handling:** Stores resulting vectors and logs in designated output directories\r\n4. **Status Reporting:** Writes job status and errors to spool or log files for auditability\r\n\r\n### Example Invocation\r\n```powershell\r\npowershell -File C:/miratv_ingest/workers/embedding_pipeline.ps1 -InputFile processed/series_42.json -Model embed-english-v3.0\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All embedding jobs are logged for traceability\r\n- No direct database writes; outputs are staged for ingestion by downstream workers\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial results (unknowns are preserved)\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** embedding_pipeline_worker\r\n- **domain:** content_enrichment\r\n- **topic:** embedding_vectorization\r\n- **unit_type:** worker\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check input file paths and permissions\r\n- Review logs in `reports/` or `tmp/` for error details\r\n- Ensure downstream embedding services are reachable\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:57:36', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

This script is responsible for aggregating operational metrics, error events, and performance data, then forwarding them to the appropriate reporting or logging endpoints.\r\n\r\n### Location\r\n`C:/miratv_ingest/telemetry_watcher.ps1`\r\n\r\n### Operational Context\r\n- **Domain:** Telemetry / Monitoring\r\n- **Trigger:** Manual, scheduled, or orchestrated by pipeline spine\r\n- **Inputs:** Log files, spool files, or direct worker output\r\n- **Outputs:** Aggregated telemetry reports, status logs, and event notifications\r\n- **Downstream:** May post to server telemetry endpoints or local audit logs\r\n\r\n### Usage Pattern\r\n- Run periodically or in response to pipeline events\r\n- Can be invoked by orchestration scripts or as a standalone monitor\r\n- Supports parameterized input (e.g., target log, time window)\r\n\r\n### Key Steps\r\n1. **Data Collection:** Reads logs, spools, or worker outputs for telemetry events\r\n2. **Aggregation:** Summarizes metrics (counts, errors, durations)\r\n3. **Reporting:** Sends telemetry summaries to server or writes to local logs\r\n4. **Alerting:** Optionally triggers notifications on error thresholds\r\n\r\n### Example Invocation\r\n```powershell\r\npowershell -File C:/miratv_ingest/telemetry_watcher.ps1 -LogFile reports/pipeline.log -Window 24h\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All telemetry events are logged for auditability\r\n- No direct database writes; reporting is append-only\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial data\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** telemetry_watcher_worker\r\n- **domain:** telemetry\r\n- **topic:** pipeline_monitoring\r\n- **unit_type:** worker\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check log file paths and permissions\r\n- Review output logs for error details\r\n- Ensure server endpoints are reachable if remote reporting is enabled\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:57:55', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

C:/miratv_ingest/shared/simple_log.ps1\r\nWrite-Log -Message \'Pipeline started\' -Level \'INFO\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All log entries are append-only for auditability\r\n- No direct database writes; logs are local only\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial data\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** shared_simple_log_utility\r\n- **domain:** logging\r\n- **topic:** shared_utilities\r\n- **unit_type:** module\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check calling script for correct import\r\n- Review log file permissions and disk space\r\n- Ensure log rotation settings are appropriate\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:59:38', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

(67, 'upload_spool_once_utility', 'signal_spool', 'data_upload', 'utility', '# MiraTV Spool Uploader Utility Guide\r\n\r\n## Component: upload_spool_once.ps1\r\n\r\n### Purpose\r\nPerforms a one-time upload of a specified spool file (event, telemetry, or governance signal) to the server or designated endpoint. Used for ad-hoc or manual uploads outside of scheduled or batch processes.\r\n\r\n### Location\r\n`C:/miratv_ingest/upload_spool_once.ps1`\r\n\r\n### Operational Context\r\n- **Domain:** Signal Spool / Data Upload\r\n- **Trigger:** Manual, ad-hoc\r\n- **Inputs:** Single spool file (e.g., from `igm_spool/`, `lake_spool/`, `ops_spool/`)\r\n- **Outputs:** Uploaded data to server endpoint, status log\r\n- **Downstream:** Server-side aggregators, registry, or audit logs\r\n\r\n### Usage Pattern\r\n- Run manually for a specific file needing upload\r\n- Supports parameterized input (e.g., file path, target endpoint)\r\n\r\n### Key Steps\r\n1. **Input Validation:** Checks that the specified file exists and is readable\r\n2. **Upload:** Transfers the file to the server via HTTP POST or SCP\r\n3. **Status Logging:** Records upload status and errors\r\n\r\n### Example Invocation\r\n```powershell\r\npowershell -File C:/miratv_ingest/upload_spool_once.ps1 -File igm_spool/event_20260202.log -Endpoint https://miratv.club/_ingest/upload_spool.php\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All uploads are logged for traceability\r\n- No direct database writes; uploads are append-only\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial uploads\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** upload_spool_once_utility\r\n- **domain:** signal_spool\r\n- **topic:** data_upload\r\n- **unit_type:** utility\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check file path and permissions\r\n- Review status log for error details\r\n- Ensure server endpoint is reachable\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 15:02:19', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

Governance Restriction\r\n**This endpoint is intended for AI agent, admin, and local automation use.**\r\nFor all other access patterns, refer to CVI documentation and (when available) stored procedure communication guides for proper integration.\r\n\r\n## Purpose\r\nThis guide explains how to use the Dog_open.php endpoint (CVI) to communicate with registry databases, including uploading and retrieving instructions or operational metadata.\r\n\r\n\r\n## 1. Endpoint\r\n- **URL:** https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\r\n- **Method:** HTTP POST\r\n- **Content-Type:** application/json\r\n- **Authentication:** token (required)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 2. Uploading Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with these fields:\r\n- `token`: Your ingest token\r\n- `db`: Target database (e.g., PCDE_memory)\r\n- `sql`: Parameterized SQL (use ? for values)\r\n- `params`: Array of values for the SQL statement\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"INSERT INTO pcde_procedure_registry (process_name, domain, topic, unit_type, instruction, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW());\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\', \'governance\', \'cvi_access\', \'guide\', \'How to use Dog_open.php for direct, governed DB access. POST JSON: token, db, sql, params. SQL must be parameterized. All actions are logged and auditable.\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 3. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n- **Direct use is restricted to AI/admin/automation only.**\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. Governance Restriction\r\n**This endpoint is intended for AI agent, admin, and local automation use.**\r\nFor all other access patterns, refer to CVI documentation and (when available) stored procedure communication guides for proper integration.\r\n\r\n## Purpose\r\nThis guide explains how to use the Dog_open.php endpoint (CVI) to communicate with registry databases, including uploading and retrieving instructions or operational metadata.\r\n\r\n\r\n## 1. Endpoint\r\n- **URL:** https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\r\n- **Method:** HTTP POST\r\n- **Content-Type:** application/json\r\n- **Authentication:** token (required)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 2. Uploading Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with these fields:\r\n- `token`: Your ingest token\r\n- `db`: Target database (e.g., PCDE_memory)\r\n- `sql`: Parameterized SQL (use ? for values)\r\n- `params`: Array of values for the SQL statement\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"INSERT INTO pcde_procedure_registry (process_name, domain, topic, unit_type, instruction, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW());\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\', \'governance\', \'cvi_access\', \'guide\', \'How to use Dog_open.php for direct, governed DB access. POST JSON: token, db, sql, params. SQL must be parameterized. All actions are logged and auditable.\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 3. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n- **Direct use is restricted to AI/admin/automation only.**\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. Governance Restriction\r\n**This endpoint is intended for AI agent, admin, and local automation use.**\r\nFor all other access patterns, refer to CVI documentation and (when available) stored procedure communication guides for proper integration.\r\n\r\n## Purpose\r\nThis guide explains how to use the Dog_open.php endpoint (CVI) to communicate with registry databases, including uploading and retrieving instructions or operational metadata.\r\n\r\n\r\n## 1. Endpoint\r\n- **URL:** https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\r\n- **Method:** HTTP POST\r\n- **Content-Type:** application/json\r\n- **Authentication:** token (required)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 2. Uploading Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with these fields:\r\n- `token`: Your ingest token\r\n- `db`: Target database (e.g., PCDE_memory)\r\n- `sql`: Parameterized SQL (use ? for values)\r\n- `params`: Array of values for the SQL statement\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"INSERT INTO pcde_procedure_registry (process_name, domain, topic, unit_type, instruction, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW());\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\', \'governance\', \'cvi_access\', \'guide\', \'How to use Dog_open.php for direct, governed DB access. POST JSON: token, db, sql, params. SQL must be parameterized. All actions are logged and auditable.\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 3. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n- **Direct use is restricted to AI/admin/automation only.**\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. (121, 'dog_open_usage', 'governance', 'cvi_access', 'guide', '# How to Use Dog_open.php (CVI) for Registry Communication\r\n\r\n## Purpose\r\nThis guide explains how to use the Dog_open.php endpoint (CVI) to communicate with registry databases, including uploading and retrieving instructions or operational metadata.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 1. Endpoint\r\n- **URL:** https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\r\n- **Method:** HTTP POST\r\n- **Content-Type:** application/json\r\n- **Authentication:** token (required)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 2. Uploading Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with these fields:\r\n- `token`: Your ingest token\r\n- `db`: Target database (e.g., PCDE_memory)\r\n- `sql`: Parameterized SQL (use ? for values)\r\n- `params`: Array of values for the SQL statement\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"INSERT INTO pcde_procedure_registry (process_name, domain, topic, unit_type, instruction, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW());\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\', \'governance\', \'cvi_access\', \'guide\', \'How to use Dog_open.php for direct, governed DB access. POST JSON: token, db, sql, params. SQL must be parameterized. All actions are logged and auditable.\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 3. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. Each step is a dedicated script, operating on files only (no DB writes), producing intermediate JSON artifacts for later ingestion.\r\n\r\n## Key Scripts & Steps\r\n- `series_grinder.ps1` – Extracts core series fields from raw payloads\r\n- `series_grinder_2_series_ext.ps1` – Extracts extended series metadata\r\n- `series_grinder_3_seasons.ps1` – Extracts season units by structure\r\n- `series_grinder_4_season_ext.ps1` – Extracts extended season metadata\r\n- `series_grinder_5_episodes.ps1` – Extracts episode units, supports fallback for season-keyed objects\r\n- `series_grinder_6_cleaner.ps1` – Cleans up processed files and removes raw artifacts\r\n- `series_grinder_7_finalizer.ps1` – (Empty/placeholder for future finalization)\r\n- `series_grinder_arrays.ps1` – Handles array-based series payloads, repairs display wrapping\r\n\r\n## Key Workflows\r\n- Each script reads from `raw_store/pickup/default` and writes to `series_sep/`\r\n- Extraction is anchor-based, not schema-based (brace/bracket block parsing)\r\n- No DB access; all operations are file-based for safety and traceability\r\n- Cleaning step removes all intermediate and raw artifacts\r\n\r\n## Integration Points\r\n- Downstream: Normalizer and ingest workers\r\n- Upstream: Provider payload downloaders\r\n\r\n## CVI/Registry Notes\r\n- All scripts are modular and CVI-explicit for registry onboarding\r\n- Each step is independently runnable for debugging\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## Actionable Onboarding\r\n- Run: Execute each script in order for a full pipeline\r\n- Registry: All modules are CVI-ready for PCDE_memory onboarding\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:49:07', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

(170, 'embedding_pipeline_worker', 'content_enrichment', 'embedding_vectorization', 'worker', '# MiraTV Embedding Pipeline Worker Guide\r\n\r\n## Component: embedding_pipeline.ps1\r\n\r\n### Purpose\r\nAutomates the embedding pipeline for series, VOD, or live content in the MiraTV ingest system. This worker script is responsible for triggering embedding jobs, managing input/output files, and coordinating with downstream AI or vectorization services.\r\n\r\n### Location\r\n`C:/miratv_ingest/workers/embedding_pipeline.ps1`\r\n\r\n### Operational Context\r\n- **Domain:** Content Enrichment / Vectorization\r\n- **Trigger:** Manual or orchestrated via spine scheduler or batch triggers\r\n- **Inputs:** Processed content files (JSON, text, or other supported formats)\r\n- **Outputs:** Embedding vectors, logs, and status reports (typically in `processed/` or `tmp/`)\r\n- **Downstream:** May call external AI embedding APIs (Cohere, OpenAI) or local embedding workers\r\n\r\n### Usage Pattern\r\n- Run as part of the enrichment phase after grinder/normalization\r\n- Can be invoked directly or by orchestration scripts in `triggers/` or `spine/`\r\n- Supports parameterized input (e.g., target file, embedding model)\r\n\r\n### Key Steps\r\n1. **Input Validation:** Checks for required input files and parameters\r\n2. **Embedding Job Launch:** Calls embedding service or script, passing content for vectorization\r\n3. **Output Handling:** Stores resulting vectors and logs in designated output directories\r\n4. **Status Reporting:** Writes job status and errors to spool or log files for auditability\r\n\r\n### Example Invocation\r\n```powershell\r\npowershell -File C:/miratv_ingest/workers/embedding_pipeline.ps1 -InputFile processed/series_42.json -Model embed-english-v3.0\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All embedding jobs are logged for traceability\r\n- No direct database writes; outputs are staged for ingestion by downstream workers\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial results (unknowns are preserved)\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** embedding_pipeline_worker\r\n- **domain:** content_enrichment\r\n- **topic:** embedding_vectorization\r\n- **unit_type:** worker\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check input file paths and permissions\r\n- Review logs in `reports/` or `tmp/` for error details\r\n- Ensure downstream embedding services are reachable\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:57:36', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

(172, 'telemetry_watcher_worker', 'telemetry', 'pipeline_monitoring', 'worker', '# MiraTV Telemetry Watcher Worker Guide\r\n\r\n## Component: telemetry_watcher.ps1\r\n\r\n### Purpose\r\nMonitors and collects telemetry data from various pipeline stages and workers in the MiraTV ingest system. This script is responsible for aggregating operational metrics, error events, and performance data, then forwarding them to the appropriate reporting or logging endpoints.\r\n\r\n### Location\r\n`C:/miratv_ingest/telemetry_watcher.ps1`\r\n\r\n### Operational Context\r\n- **Domain:** Telemetry / Monitoring\r\n- **Trigger:** Manual, scheduled, or orchestrated by pipeline spine\r\n- **Inputs:** Log files, spool files, or direct worker output\r\n- **Outputs:** Aggregated telemetry reports, status logs, and event notifications\r\n- **Downstream:** May post to server telemetry endpoints or local audit logs\r\n\r\n### Usage Pattern\r\n- Run periodically or in response to pipeline events\r\n- Can be invoked by orchestration scripts or as a standalone monitor\r\n- Supports parameterized input (e.g., target log, time window)\r\n\r\n### Key Steps\r\n1. **Data Collection:** Reads logs, spools, or worker outputs for telemetry events\r\n2. **Aggregation:** Summarizes metrics (counts, errors, durations)\r\n3. **Reporting:** Sends telemetry summaries to server or writes to local logs\r\n4. **Alerting:** Optionally triggers notifications on error thresholds\r\n\r\n### Example Invocation\r\n```powershell\r\npowershell -File C:/miratv_ingest/telemetry_watcher.ps1 -LogFile reports/pipeline.log -Window 24h\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All telemetry events are logged for auditability\r\n- No direct database writes; reporting is append-only\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial data\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** telemetry_watcher_worker\r\n- **domain:** telemetry\r\n- **topic:** pipeline_monitoring\r\n- **unit_type:** worker\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check log file paths and permissions\r\n- Review output logs for error details\r\n- Ensure server endpoints are reachable if remote reporting is enabled\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:57:55', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

Ensures that all relevant signal data is transferred for aggregation, audit, and downstream processing.\r\n\r\n### Location\r\n`C:/miratv_ingest/spool_uploader.ps1`\r\n\r\n### Operational Context\r\n- **Domain:** Signal Spool / Data Upload\r\n- **Trigger:** Manual, scheduled, or orchestrated by pipeline spine\r\n- **Inputs:** Spool files (e.g., `igm_spool/`, `lake_spool/`, `ops_spool/`)\r\n- **Outputs:** Uploaded data to server endpoints, status logs\r\n- **Downstream:** Server-side aggregators, registry, or audit logs\r\n\r\n### Usage Pattern\r\n- Run periodically or after batch processing completes\r\n- Can be invoked by orchestration scripts or as a standalone uploader\r\n- Supports parameterized input (e.g., spool type, target endpoint)\r\n\r\n### Key Steps\r\n1. **Spool Discovery:** Identifies new or unuploaded spool files\r\n2. **Upload:** Transfers files to server via HTTP POST or SCP\r\n3. **Status Logging:** Records upload status and errors\r\n4. **Cleanup:** Optionally archives or deletes successfully uploaded files\r\n\r\n### Example Invocation\r\n```powershell\r\npowershell -File C:/miratv_ingest/spool_uploader.ps1 -SpoolDir igm_spool/ -Endpoint https://miratv.club/_ingest/upload_spool.php\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Governance & Compliance\r\n- All uploads are logged for traceability\r\n- No direct database writes; uploads are append-only\r\n- Follows fail-open policy for partial uploads\r\n\r\n### CVI/Registry Metadata\r\n- **process_name:** spool_uploader_worker\r\n- **domain:** signal_spool\r\n- **topic:** data_upload\r\n- **unit_type:** worker\r\n\r\n### Troubleshooting\r\n- Check spool directory paths and permissions\r\n- Review status logs for error details\r\n- Ensure server endpoints are reachable\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Last updated:** 2026-02-02\r\n', '2026-02-02 14:58:11', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

(200, 'how_to_use_dog_open_cvi', 'misc', 'misc', 'misc', '\r\n# How to Use Dog_open.php (CVI) for Registry Communication\r\n\r\n\r\n## ?? Governance Restriction\r\n**This endpoint is intended for AI agent, admin, and local automation use.**\r\nFor all other access patterns, refer to CVI documentation and (when available) stored procedure communication guides for proper integration.\r\n\r\n## Purpose\r\nThis guide explains how to use the Dog_open.php endpoint (CVI) to communicate with registry databases, including uploading and retrieving instructions or operational metadata.\r\n\r\n\r\n## 1. Endpoint\r\n- **URL:** https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\r\n- **Method:** HTTP POST\r\n- **Content-Type:** application/json\r\n- **Authentication:** token (required)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 2. Uploading Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with these fields:\r\n- `token`: Your ingest token\r\n- `db`: Target database (e.g., PCDE_memory)\r\n- `sql`: Parameterized SQL (use ? for values)\r\n- `params`: Array of values for the SQL statement\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"INSERT INTO pcde_procedure_registry (process_name, domain, topic, unit_type, instruction, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW());\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\', \'governance\', \'cvi_access\', \'guide\', \'How to use Dog_open.php for direct, governed DB access. POST JSON: token, db, sql, params. SQL must be parameterized. All actions are logged and auditable.\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 3. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n- **Direct use is restricted to AI/admin/automation only.**\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. Contact\r\nFor endpoint or schema issues, contact the system architect or registry owner.\r\n', '2026-02-02 15:31:35', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

Flow Overview\r\n1. Fetch pending embeddings from DB\r\n2. Batch embed with Cohere\r\n3. Store results in DB\r\n4. Upload registry entry (CVI)\r\n5. Record telemetry\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Key Files\r\n- embedding_pipeline.ps1 (main logic)\r\n- telemetry.ps1 (shared telemetry module)\r\n- pcde_procedure_registry_create.sql (registry schema)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n- **Direct use is restricted to AI/admin/automation only.**\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. (221, 'how_to_use_dog_open_cvi', 'misc', 'misc', 'misc', '\r\n# How to Use Dog_open.php (CVI) for Registry Communication\r\n\r\n\r\n## ?? Governance Restriction\r\n**This endpoint is intended for AI agent, admin, and local automation use.**\r\nFor all other access patterns, refer to CVI documentation and (when available) stored procedure communication guides for proper integration.\r\n\r\n## Purpose\r\nThis guide explains how to use the Dog_open.php endpoint (CVI) to communicate with registry databases, including uploading and retrieving instructions or operational metadata.\r\n\r\n\r\n## 1. Endpoint\r\n- **URL:** https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\r\n- **Method:** HTTP POST\r\n- **Content-Type:** application/json\r\n- **Authentication:** token (required)\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 2. Uploading Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with these fields:\r\n- `token`: Your ingest token\r\n- `db`: Target database (e.g., PCDE_memory)\r\n- `sql`: Parameterized SQL (use ? for values)\r\n- `params`: Array of values for the SQL statement\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"INSERT INTO pcde_procedure_registry (process_name, domain, topic, unit_type, instruction, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW());\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\', \'governance\', \'cvi_access\', \'guide\', \'How to use Dog_open.php for direct, governed DB access. POST JSON: token, db, sql, params. SQL must be parameterized. All actions are logged and auditable.\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 3. Retrieving Data (Example)\r\nSend a JSON body with a SELECT statement:\r\n- `sql`: e.g., \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n- `params`: e.g., @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n\r\n### Example PowerShell\r\n```\r\n$body = @{\r\n    token = \'YOUR_TOKEN\'\r\n    db    = \'PCDE_memory\'\r\n    sql   = \"SELECT * FROM pcde_procedure_registry WHERE process_name = ?;\"\r\n    params = @(\'dog_open_usage\')\r\n} | ConvertTo-Json\r\n\r\nInvoke-RestMethod -Uri \'https://miratv.club/_workers/api/series/dog_open.php\' -Method Post -Body $body -ContentType \'application/json\'\r\n```\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 4. Security & Audit\r\n- All actions require a valid token.\r\n- All SQL must be parameterized (no direct string interpolation).\r\n- All actions are logged and auditable by system governance.\r\n- **Direct use is restricted to AI/admin/automation only.**\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 5. Troubleshooting\r\n- 403 Forbidden: Check your token.\r\n- Table not found: Ensure the table exists in the target DB.\r\n- SQL error: Check your SQL and params for correctness.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## 6. Contact\r\nFor endpoint or schema issues, contact the system architect or registry owner.\r\n', '2026-02-03 09:33:27', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),

Each step is a dedicated script, operating on files only (no DB writes), producing intermediate JSON artifacts for later ingestion.\r\n\r\n## Key Scripts & Steps\r\n- `series_grinder.ps1` – Extracts core series fields from raw payloads\r\n- `series_grinder_2_series_ext.ps1` – Extracts extended series metadata\r\n- `series_grinder_3_seasons.ps1` – Extracts season units by structure\r\n- `series_grinder_4_season_ext.ps1` – Extracts extended season metadata\r\n- `series_grinder_5_episodes.ps1` – Extracts episode units, supports fallback for season-keyed objects\r\n- `series_grinder_6_cleaner.ps1` – Cleans up processed files and removes raw artifacts\r\n- `series_grinder_7_finalizer.ps1` – (Empty/placeholder for future finalization)\r\n- `series_grinder_arrays.ps1` – Handles array-based series payloads, repairs display wrapping\r\n\r\n## Key Workflows\r\n- Each script reads from `raw_store/pickup/default` and writes to `series_sep/`\r\n- Extraction is anchor-based, not schema-based (brace/bracket block parsing)\r\n- No DB access; all operations are file-based for safety and traceability\r\n- Cleaning step removes all intermediate and raw artifacts\r\n\r\n## Integration Points\r\n- Downstream: Normalizer and ingest workers\r\n- Upstream: Provider payload downloaders\r\n\r\n## CVI/Registry Notes\r\n- All scripts are modular and CVI-explicit for registry onboarding\r\n- Each step is independently runnable for debugging\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n## Actionable Onboarding\r\n- Run: Execute each script in order for a full pipeline\r\n- Registry: All modules are CVI-ready for PCDE_memory onboarding\r\n', '2026-02-03 09:33:35', 'admin', NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL),
